The film received an [Oscar nomination](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/91st_Academy_Awards "wikipedia:91st Academy Awards") for "[Best Visual Effects](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Visual_Effects "wikipedia:Academy Award for Best Visual Effects"),"[[71]](#cite_note-Oscar_nomination-71) and a [Saturn](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saturn_Award "wikipedia:Saturn Award") nomination for "Best Science Fiction Film Release."[[72]](#cite_note-72)

## Adaptations and tie-in media[]

 [![Alden Ehrenreich as Han Solo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/HanSolo10BBY-SoloOMG.png/revision/latest?cb=20241220234455) [![Alden Ehrenreich as Han Solo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/HanSolo10BBY-SoloOMG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20241220234455)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/HanSolo10BBY-SoloOMG.png/revision/latest?cb=20241220234455) 

Alden Ehrenreich as Han Solo

 

Lucasfilm arranged *Solo* licensing deals with [Denny's](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Denny%27s "wikipedia:Denny's"), [Esurance](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Esurance "wikipedia:Esurance"), [General Mills](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_Mills "wikipedia:General Mills"), [Nissan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nissan "wikipedia:Nissan"), [Solo Cup Company](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Solo_Cup_Company "wikipedia:Solo Cup Company") and [Symantec](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Symantec "wikipedia:Symantec").[[73]](#cite_note-73) Denny's aired a commercial that utilized props, characters and a set from the film.[[74]](#cite_note-Denny's-74) The French car company [Renault](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Renault "wikipedia:Renault") also aired an ad showcasing the film's train sequence.[[75]](#cite_note-75) The *Solo* merchandise line debuted in stores on [April 13](/wiki/April_13 "April 13").[[76]](#cite_note-Products_Revealed-76) The video games *[Star Wars Battlefront II](/wiki/Star_Wars_Battlefront_II "Star Wars Battlefront II")*, *[Star Wars: Commander](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Commander "Star Wars: Commander")*, *[Star Wars: Force Arena](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Force_Arena "Star Wars: Force Arena")*, *[Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galaxy_of_Heroes "Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes")*, *[Star Wars Pinball](/wiki/Star_Wars_Pinball "Star Wars Pinball")* and *[Minecraft](/wiki/Minecraft "Minecraft")* were updated with *Solo*-related content.[[77]](#cite_note-Solo_season-77)[[78]](#cite_note-SW-Updated:_Star_Wars_Games_Are_Getting_Special_Modifications_with_New_Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Content-78)[[79]](#cite_note-SW-Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Blasts_Into_Pinball_FX3_-_Exclusive-79)[[80]](#cite_note-SW-Tips_for_Building_the_Millennium_Falcon_in_Minecraft-80) Various [LEGO](/wiki/LEGO "LEGO") sets were released as part of LEGO's overall *[LEGO Star Wars](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars "LEGO Star Wars")* line, creating the *[LEGO Star Wars Solo](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars_Solo "LEGO Star Wars Solo")* subtheme.[[81]](#cite_note-LegoSolo-81)

Tie-in stories to *Solo* included the novel *[Last Shot](/wiki/Last_Shot "Last Shot")* by [Daniel José Older](/wiki/Daniel_Jos%C3%A9_Older "Daniel José Older"), the comic *[Star Wars: Lando - Double or Nothing](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Lando_-_Double_or_Nothing "Star Wars: Lando - Double or Nothing")*,[[82]](#cite_note-New_Books_and_Comic-82) and the novel *[Most Wanted](/wiki/Most_Wanted "Most Wanted")*, which is set during Han and Qi'ra's days on Corellia and sets up their desire to escape.[[83]](#cite_note-Most_Wanted-83) On the same day as the film's release,[[84]](#cite_note-Penguin-84) the *[Solo: A Star Wars Story The Official Guide](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story_The_Official_Guide "Solo: A Star Wars Story The Official Guide")* by [Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo") was released, identifying many of the background elements and characters from the film.[[85]](#cite_note-SoloOG-85) Other reference materials released in promotion of the film included *[The Official Movie Guide](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story_-_The_Official_Movie_Guide "Solo: A Star Wars Story - The Official Movie Guide")*,[[86]](#cite_note-Official_Guide-86) *[Entertainment Weekly's The Ultimate Guide to Han Solo](/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly%27s_The_Ultimate_Guide_to_Han_Solo "Entertainment Weekly's The Ultimate Guide to Han Solo")*,[[87]](#cite_note-EW_Solo_Guide-87) *[Solo: A Star Wars Story Ultimate Sticker Collection](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Ultimate_Sticker_Collection "Solo: A Star Wars Story Ultimate Sticker Collection")*,[[88]](#cite_note-Sticker-88) and *[Star Wars Insider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider")*'s "[Soldiers of the Empire](/wiki/Soldiers_of_the_Empire:_Policing_the_Worlds_of_Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story "Soldiers of the Empire: Policing the Worlds of Solo: A Star Wars Story")" article.[[89]](#cite_note-181_Soldiers-89) The book *[The Art of Solo: A Star Wars Story](/wiki/The_Art_of_Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story "The Art of Solo: A Star Wars Story")* detailed the behind the scenes development of the film from a concept art perspective.[[90]](#cite_note-Art_of-90) *[Solo: A Star Wars Story: The Ultimate Guide](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story:_The_Ultimate_Guide "Solo: A Star Wars Story: The Ultimate Guide")* was later released as another behind the scenes text.[[91]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Guide-91)

### Lawsuits[]

The release of the initial teaser posters prompted a complaint from a French artist, Hachim Bahous, that the design of the posters was a plagiarization of a series of covers he designed for Sony Music for French album releases. A side-by-side post demonstrated that the posters and covers feature nearly identical coloration for both the background and character/album names, as well as a similar font.[[92]](#cite_note-gamespot-92)[[93]](#cite_note-Hollywood_Reporter_March_2018-93)[[94]](#cite_note-indiewire-94) On [April 23](/wiki/April_23 "April 23"), a lawsuit was filed by Ren Ventures, who holds the trademark for the card game Sabacc, against Lucasfilm and Denny's *Star Wars* card game after Sabacc was featured in promotion for the film.[[95]](#cite_note-95)

### Home video[]

*Solo* was released on digital streaming formats on [September 14](/wiki/September_14 "September 14"), and on physical media and on-demand on [September 25](/wiki/September_25 "September 25").[[96]](#cite_note-SW-Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Makes_the_Jump_Home-96)

Bonus features:

* Solo: The Director & Cast Roundtable — Sit down with director Ron Howard and the stars for an intimate and entertaining discussion of the film's making.
* Team Chewie — See what it takes to bring your favorite Wookiee to life in this lighthearted look behind the scenes.
* Kasdan on Kasdan — Iconic Star Wars screenwriter Lawrence Kasdan and son Jonathan share what it was like to write the movie's script together.
* Remaking the Millennium Falcon — Track the transformation of the most famous ship in the galaxy, from Lando's swank and impeccable pride and joy to Han's stripped-down hot-rod freighter with "special modifications."
* Escape from Corellia — Get behind the wheel for the making of this high-octane chase through the streets of Corellia.
* [The Train Heist](/wiki/The_Train_Heist "The Train Heist") — Explore the challenges and thrills of creating this action-packed sequence, including its remote location and spectacular effects.
* Becoming a Droid: L3-37 — Meet the newest droid—and the talented actor who helps bring her to life.
* [Scoundrels, Droids, Creatures and Cards: Welcome to Fort Ypso](/wiki/Scoundrels,_Droids,_Creatures_and_Cards:_Welcome_to_Fort_Ypso "Scoundrels, Droids, Creatures and Cards: Welcome to Fort Ypso") — Take an in-depth tour of the rough-and-tumble bar where strangers mix and gamblers risk all in the legendary card game, Sabacc.
* Into the Maelstrom: The Kessel Run — Join Han and Chewie at the controls of the Millennium Falcon to see how this legendary moment in Star Wars history unfolds.
* The Millennium Falcon: From Page to Park — In an exclusive bonus feature available as a digital code with the Target release, you can get a look at the history of the most famous ship in the galaxy, its origin and development, and how it will translate in one of the most anticipated expansions in [Disneyland](/wiki/Disneyland "Disneyland")'s history.
* Deleted Scenes: Proxima's Den, Corellian Foot Chase, Han Solo: Imperial Cadet, The Battle of Mimban: Extended, Han Versus Chewie: Extended, Snowball Fight!, Meet Dryden: Extended, Coaxium Double-Cross

On the day of the digital streaming release, co-writer Jon Kasdan posted 52 behind the scenes details (in lieu of an audio commentary) on his Twitter account.[[97]](#cite_note-97) He later joined [Ray Park](/wiki/Ray_Park "Ray Park") and the hosts of *[The Star Wars Show](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Show "The Star Wars Show")* for a Facebook live preview of the film's bonus features.[[98]](#cite_note-SW-The_Star_Wars_Show_Meets_Solo_for_a_Special_Facebook_Event-98)[[99]](#cite_note-99)

**[Jerome Blake](/wiki/Jerome_Blake "Jerome Blake")** as Unknown role[[105]](#cite_note-105)   Aside from his credited role, Warwick Davis also played characters in the Sabacc and droid rebellion scenes, and acted as advisor for various droids and creatures.[[106]](#cite_note-106)  Screenwriter [Jon Kasdan](/wiki/Jon_Kasdan "Jon Kasdan") and first assistant director [Toby Hefferman](/wiki/Toby_Hefferman "Toby Hefferman") filmed a scene as [Tag Greenley](/wiki/Tag_Greenley "Tag Greenley") and [Bink Otauna](/wiki/Bink_Otauna "Bink Otauna"), two characters that first appeared in the [*Star Wars* comics](/wiki/Star_Wars_comic_books "Star Wars comic books") published by [Dark Horse Comics](/wiki/Dark_Horse_Comics "Dark Horse Comics").[[107]](#cite_note-107) However, this was deleted from the final cut of the film.[[28]](#cite_note-Interesting_Bits-28)[[108]](#cite_note-108)  Jerome Blake who previously played many roles in the [Prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy") including [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") among other characters, shot scenes for the film that were ultimately deleted. It is unknown if the appearance was a reprisal of Amedda, another previous role or a new one made for the film.[[109]](#cite_note-109) |
